        <td id="L40" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="40"></td>
        <td id="LC40" class="blob-code js-file-line">CHAPTER I. Down the Rabbit-Hole</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L41" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="41"></td>
        <td id="LC41" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L42" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="42"></td>
        <td id="LC42" class="blob-code js-file-line">Alice was beginning to get very tired of sitting by her sister on the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L43" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="43"></td>
        <td id="LC43" class="blob-code js-file-line">bank, and of having nothing to do: once or twice she had peeped into the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L44" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="44"></td>
        <td id="LC44" class="blob-code js-file-line">book her sister was reading, but it had no pictures or conversations in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L45" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="45"></td>
        <td id="LC45" class="blob-code js-file-line">it, &#39;and what is the use of a book,&#39; thought Alice &#39;without pictures or</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L46" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="46"></td>
        <td id="LC46" class="blob-code js-file-line">conversation?&#39;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L47" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="47"></td>
        <td id="LC47" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L48" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="48"></td>
        <td id="LC48" class="blob-code js-file-line">So she was considering in her own mind (as well as she could, for the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L49" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="49"></td>
        <td id="LC49" class="blob-code js-file-line">hot day made her feel very sleepy and stupid), whether the pleasure</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L50" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="50"></td>
        <td id="LC50" class="blob-code js-file-line">of making a daisy-chain would be worth the trouble of getting up and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L51" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="51"></td>
        <td id="LC51" class="blob-code js-file-line">picking the daisies, when suddenly a White Rabbit with pink eyes ran</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L52" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="52"></td>
        <td id="LC52" class="blob-code js-file-line">close by her.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L53" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="53"></td>
        <td id="LC53" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L54" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="54"></td>
        <td id="LC54" class="blob-code js-file-line">There was nothing so VERY remarkable in that; nor did Alice think it so</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L55" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="55"></td>
        <td id="LC55" class="blob-code js-file-line">VERY much out of the way to hear the Rabbit say to itself, &#39;Oh dear!</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L56" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="56"></td>
        <td id="LC56" class="blob-code js-file-line">Oh dear! I shall be late!&#39; (when she thought it over afterwards, it</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L57" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="57"></td>
        <td id="LC57" class="blob-code js-file-line">occurred to her that she ought to have wondered at this, but at the time</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L58" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="58"></td>
        <td id="LC58" class="blob-code js-file-line">it all seemed quite natural); but when the Rabbit actually TOOK A WATCH</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L59" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="59"></td>
        <td id="LC59" class="blob-code js-file-line">OUT OF ITS WAISTCOAT-POCKET, and looked at it, and then hurried on,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L60" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="60"></td>
        <td id="LC60" class="blob-code js-file-line">Alice started to her feet, for it flashed across her mind that she had</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L61" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="61"></td>
        <td id="LC61" class="blob-code js-file-line">never before seen a rabbit with either a waistcoat-pocket, or a watch</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L62" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="62"></td>
        <td id="LC62" class="blob-code js-file-line">to take out of it, and burning with curiosity, she ran across the field</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L63" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="63"></td>
        <td id="LC63" class="blob-code js-file-line">after it, and fortunately was just in time to see it pop down a large</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L64" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="64"></td>
        <td id="LC64" class="blob-code js-file-line">rabbit-hole under the hedge.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L65" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="65"></td>
        <td id="LC65" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L66" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="66"></td>
        <td id="LC66" class="blob-code js-file-line">In another moment down went Alice after it, never once considering how</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L67" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="67"></td>
        <td id="LC67" class="blob-code js-file-line">in the world she was to get out again.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L68" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="68"></td>
        <td id="LC68" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L69" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="69"></td>
        <td id="LC69" class="blob-code js-file-line">The rabbit-hole went straight on like a tunnel for some way, and then</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L70" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="70"></td>
        <td id="LC70" class="blob-code js-file-line">dipped suddenly down, so suddenly that Alice had not a moment to think</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L71" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="71"></td>
        <td id="LC71" class="blob-code js-file-line">about stopping herself before she found herself falling down a very deep</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L72" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="72"></td>
        <td id="LC72" class="blob-code js-file-line">well.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L73" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="73"></td>
        <td id="LC73" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L74" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="74"></td>
        <td id="LC74" class="blob-code js-file-line">Either the well was very deep, or she fell very slowly, for she had</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L75" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="75"></td>
        <td id="LC75" class="blob-code js-file-line">plenty of time as she went down to look about her and to wonder what was</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L76" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="76"></td>
        <td id="LC76" class="blob-code js-file-line">going to happen next. First, she tried to look down and make out what</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L77" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="77"></td>
        <td id="LC77" class="blob-code js-file-line">she was coming to, but it was too dark to see anything; then she</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L78" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="78"></td>
        <td id="LC78" class="blob-code js-file-line">looked at the sides of the well, and noticed that they were filled with</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L79" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="79"></td>
        <td id="LC79" class="blob-code js-file-line">cupboards and book-shelves; here and there she saw maps and pictures</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L80" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="80"></td>
        <td id="LC80" class="blob-code js-file-line">hung upon pegs. She took down a jar from one of the shelves as</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L81" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="81"></td>
        <td id="LC81" class="blob-code js-file-line">she passed; it was labelled &#39;ORANGE MARMALADE&#39;, but to her great</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L82" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="82"></td>
        <td id="LC82" class="blob-code js-file-line">disappointment it was empty: she did not like to drop the jar for fear</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L83" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="83"></td>
        <td id="LC83" class="blob-code js-file-line">of killing somebody, so managed to put it into one of the cupboards as</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L84" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="84"></td>
        <td id="LC84" class="blob-code js-file-line">she fell past it.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L85" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="85"></td>
        <td id="LC85" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L86" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="86"></td>
        <td id="LC86" class="blob-code js-file-line">&#39;Well!&#39; thought Alice to herself, &#39;after such a fall as this, I shall</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L87" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="87"></td>
        <td id="LC87" class="blob-code js-file-line">think nothing of tumbling down stairs! How brave they&#39;ll all think me at</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L88" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="88"></td>
        <td id="LC88" class="blob-code js-file-line">home! Why, I wouldn&#39;t say anything about it, even if I fell off the top</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L89" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="89"></td>
        <td id="LC89" class="blob-code js-file-line">of the house!&#39; (Which was very likely true.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L90" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="90"></td>
        <td id="LC90" class="blob-code js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L91" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="91"></td>
        <td id="LC91" class="blob-code js-file-line">Down, down, down. Would the fall NEVER come to an end! &#39;I wonder how</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L92" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="92"></td>
        <td id="LC92" class="blob-code js-file-line">many miles I&#39;ve fallen by this time?&#39; she said aloud. &#39;I must be getting</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L93" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="93"></td>
        <td id="LC93" class="blob-code js-file-line">somewhere near the centre of the earth. Let me see: that would be four</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L94" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="94"></td>
        <td id="LC94" class="blob-code js-file-line">thousand miles down, I think--&#39; (for, you see, Alice had learnt several</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L95" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="95"></td>
        <td id="LC95" class="blob-code js-file-line">things of this sort in her lessons in the schoolroom, and though this</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L96" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="96"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L98" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="98"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L99" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="99"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L100" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="100"></td>
        <td id="LC100" class="blob-code js-file-line">Longitude either, but thought they were nice grand words to say.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L101" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="101"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L102" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="102"></td>
        <td id="LC102" class="blob-code js-file-line">Presently she began again. &#39;I wonder if I shall fall right THROUGH the</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC103" class="blob-code js-file-line">earth! How funny it&#39;ll seem to come out among the people that walk with</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L104" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="104"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L108" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="108"></td>
        <td id="LC108" class="blob-code js-file-line">she tried to curtsey as she spoke--fancy CURTSEYING as you&#39;re falling</td>
